***надрывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:надрывать.html>надрыва́ть</a> (29262)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">над-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nad-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-рыва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ryvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надрывать.html>надрыва́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nadryvátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надорвать.html>надорва́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to tear slightly</li>
<li>to overstrain, to overtax, to undermine
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:надрывать.html>надрыва́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свои́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сила.html>си́лы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nadryvátʹ</b> svoí síly</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to overtax one's strength; knock oneself out</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:надрывать.html>надрыва́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:голос.html>го́лос</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nadryvátʹ</b> sebé gólos</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to overstrain one's voice</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:надрывать.html>надрыва́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:душа.html>душу</a> кому́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nadryvátʹ</b> dušu komú-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to rend smb's heart; harrow smb's soul</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:надрывать.html>надрыва́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:животик.html>живо́тики</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nadryvátʹ</b> živótiki</i> ― <span class="e-translation"> to split one's sides with laughter</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***надрываться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:надрываться.html>надрыва́ться</a> (11651)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надрывать.html>надрыва́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nadryvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надрываться.html>надрыва́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nadryvátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надорваться.html>надорва́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to tear slightly</li>
<li>to overstrain oneself, to exert oneself to the utmost, to knock oneself out, to bust a gut
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стан.html>ста́ну</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:еще.html>ещё</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:надрываться.html>надрыва́ться</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">stánu ja ješčó <b>nadryvátʹsja</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I don't intend to bust a gut!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:надрываться.html>надрыва́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хохот.html>хо́хота</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nadryvátʹsja</b> ot xóxota</i> ― <span class="e-translation"> split one's sides with laughter</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to shout, to cry, to cry at the top of one's lungs
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ишь.html>ишь</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:надрываться.html>надрыва́ется</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">išʹ, kak <b>nadryvájetsja</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">hasn't he got a good pair of lungs!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надрывать.html>надрыва́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nadryvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надрывать.html>надрыва́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nadryvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надорвать.html>надорва́ть</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nadorvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<ol><li>надзорщик</li>

***надстройка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:надстройка.html>надстро́йка</a> (22204)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">надстро́ить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nadstróitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надстройка.html>надстро́йка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nadstrójka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надстройка.html>надстро́йки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надстройка.html>надстро́йки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надстройка.html>надстро́ек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>raising, building on</li>
<li>superstructure, additional storey</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">philosophy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> superstructure
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:базис.html>ба́зис</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:надстройка.html>надстро́йка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bázis i nadstrójka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">basis and superstructure</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***надувать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:надувать.html>надува́ть</a> (22303)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надуть.html>наду́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nadútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надувать.html>надува́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">naduvátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надуть.html>наду́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to inflate, to puff out, to blow up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:надувать.html>надува́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:шина.html>ши́ну</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>naduvátʹ</b> šínu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to blow/pump up a tyre/tire</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:надувать.html>надува́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:воздушный.html>возду́шный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шарик.html>ша́рик</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>naduvátʹ</b> vozdúšnyj šárik</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to inflate (blow up) a balloon</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:надувать.html>надува́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:спасательный.html>спаса́тельный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жилет.html>жиле́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>naduvátʹ</b> spasátelʹnyj žilét</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to inflate the life jacket</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надувать.html>надува́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:щека.html>щёки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">naduvátʹ ščóki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to be puffed up; give oneself airs</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to drift <i>(by wind)</i></li>
<li>to give someone a chill</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to dupe, to swindle</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:надуваться.html>надува́ться</a> (25528)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надувать.html>надува́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">naduvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надуваться.html>надува́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">naduvátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надуться.html>наду́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fill out, to belly out, to swell out, to blow up, to inflate</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be puffed up</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to sulk, to pout</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надувать.html>надува́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">naduvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:надувший.html>наду́вший</a> (11044)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надувший.html>наду́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nadúvšij</span>)

***надутый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:надуть.html>наду́тый</a> (16539)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надуть.html>наду́тый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nadútyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past passive perfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надуть.html>наду́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nadútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надуть.html>наду́тый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nadútyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)наду́тее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)наду́тей</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>swollen, increased in volume</li>
<li>arrogant, haughty</li>
<li>pompous</li>
<li>disgruntled, offended, angry</li></ol>

***надуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:надуть.html>наду́ть</a> (11044)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дуть.html>ду́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надуть.html>наду́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nadútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надувать.html>надува́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to inflate, to puff out, to blow up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ветер.html>ве́тер</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:надуть.html>наду́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:парус.html>паруса́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">véter <b>nadúl</b> parusá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the sails filled out</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:надуть.html>наду́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:шина.html>ши́ну</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nadútʹ</b> šínu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to blow/pump up a tyre/tire</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:надуть.html>наду́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:воздушный.html>возду́шный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шарик.html>ша́рик</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nadútʹ</b> vozdúšnyj šárik</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to inflate (blow up) a balloon</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:надуть.html>наду́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:спасательный.html>спаса́тельный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жилет.html>жиле́т</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nadútʹ</b> spasátelʹnyj žilét</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to inflate the life jacket</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надуть.html>наду́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:губа.html>гу́бы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nadútʹ gúby</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pout</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to drift <i>(by wind)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ветер.html>ве́тром</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:надуть.html>наду́ло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сугроб.html>сугро́б</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:около.html>о́коло</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>до́ма</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vétrom <b>nadúlo</b> sugrób ókolo dóma</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the wind has drifted snow in a pile against the house</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:комната.html>ко́мнату</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:надуть.html>наду́ло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:холод.html>хо́лоду</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v kómnatu <b>nadúlo</b> xólodu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">a current of cold air chilled the room</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to give someone a chill
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:надуть.html>наду́ло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ухо.html>у́хо</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jemú <b>nadúlo</b> v úxo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the draught gave him an earache</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to dupe, to swindle</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:надуться.html>наду́ться</a> (12616)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надуть.html>наду́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nadútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надуться.html>наду́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nadútʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надуваться.html>надува́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fill out, to belly out, to swell out, to blow up, to inflate</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be puffed up</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to sulk, to pout</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надуть.html>наду́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nadútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***наедаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наедаться.html>наеда́ться</a> (31605)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">наед-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">najed-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наедаться.html>наеда́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">najedátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наесться.html>нае́сться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to eat one's fill/get one's fill, to eat plenty <i>(of)</i>

***наезд.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наезд.html>нае́зд</a> (16057)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наезжать.html>наезжа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">najezžátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наезд.html>нае́зд</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">najézd</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наезд.html>нае́зда</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наезд.html>нае́зды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наезд.html>нае́здов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>flying visit
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бывать.html>быва́ет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тут.html>тут</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:наезд.html>нае́здами</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on byvájet tut <b>najézdami</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">he runs round here occasionally</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> inroad, raid, incursion</li>
<li>running-down accident
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:совершить.html>соверши́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:наезд.html>нае́зд</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> кого́-л</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">soveršítʹ <b>najézd</b> na kovó-l</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">run down smb</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">cinematography</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> zoom-in, dollying in</li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наездник.html>нае́здник</a> (21504)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">нае́здить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">najézditʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to run over, cross, ride</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ник</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наездник.html>нае́здник</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">najézdnik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наездник.html>нае́здника</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наездник.html>нае́здники</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наездник.html>нае́здников</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">нае́здница</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>horseman, equestrian</li>
<li><i>(horse)</i> trainer, jockey</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">zoology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> ichneumon-fly</li></ol>

***наезжать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наезжать.html>наезжа́ть</a> (14897)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-езжа́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-jezžátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to go (by vehicle)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наезжать.html>наезжа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">najezžátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наехать.html>нае́хать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to run into, to hit <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + accusative, someone/something</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> imperfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to visit periodically <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + accusative, someone/something</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to come in large numbers</li>
<li>to seal, to smooth down (a road)
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">нае́здить</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">najézditʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***наехать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наехать.html>нае́хать</a> (17486)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ехать.html>е́хать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jéxatʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to go (by vehicle)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наехать.html>нае́хать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">najéxatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наезжать.html>наезжа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to run into, to hit <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:машина.html>маши́на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:наехать.html>нае́хала</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Mašína <b>najéxala</b> na nevó.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">A car ran into him.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to come in large numbers</li></ol>
